**16:50** `Missy Fizzy 🧚☘️`: ↩︎ replying to an earlier message Imagine consciousness as a kind of blockchain network. Each person’s mind is like an individual node, and reality is the shared “ledger” or record we all agree upon.

Just like in blockchain, nodes (people) achieve consensus—a shared version of truth that everyone on the network agrees to. In this case, that consensus is our shared reality or the things we all agree are "real" (society's beliefs, values, laws, etc.). You could think of these as agreed-upon delusions because they are ideas that we collectively believe in, even if they’re subjective or socially constructed.

Now, if “transcendence” is a hard fork, that means breaking away from the consensus—updating or transforming your view of reality to a new “chain” that others might not follow. A hard fork creates a new version of the blockchain, and similarly, transcending could mean a new reality or perspective that’s separate from the shared, agreed-upon one.

Chat gpts breakdown in simple terms (reactions: 👏x1)
